<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.229412s;" class="preSlide">Distinctive Outcome</h2><h4 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.238235s;" class="preFade"><strong>Beyond Primary-One readiness, </strong><span class="sqsrte-text-color--accent"><strong>we Nurture the Future </strong></span><strong>today!</strong> </h4><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.247059s;">Our commitment is to nurture every child to be a person of <strong>Good Character </strong>who is an <strong>Explorer, </strong>an <strong>Innovator</strong> and an <strong>Entrepreneur.</strong></p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.255882s;">The conviction of John Wesley, our Founder : <strong><em>The education of the heart is essential to the heart of learning</em></strong> undergirds our strong emphasis in character development based on Christian values.&nbsp;</p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.264706s;">On the foundation of a Good Character which influences a childs learning dispositions and attitude towards learning and life, we nurture every Methodist preschooler to be ready for the future, with the mindset of an:</p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.273529s;"><strong>Explorer</strong>&nbsp; ~ <em>curious, courageous and adventure-seeking to discover new ideas and concepts in the world around them</em></p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.282353s;"><strong>Innovator</strong>&nbsp; ~ <em>initiative, creativity and risk-taking through play, where they expand their understanding of their experiences and develop ideas collaboratively.</em></p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.291176s;"><strong>Entrepreneur</strong>&nbsp; ~ <em>inventive and resilient in seeking solutions to problems and not afraid to try new ideas and communicate confidently in front of others.</em></p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div></div></div></div>
    </div>
  
  </div>
  
</section>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.317647s;" class="preSlide">Integrated STEM-Based Curriculum<br><em>with Age-Appropriate Approach</em></h2><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.326471s;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--black">Our holistic</span> <strong>STEM-based curriculum</strong> <span class="sqsrte-text-color--black">(Science, Technology, Engineering and Mathematics) is enhanced with the creative integration of </span><strong>innovative education technology</strong>. <span class="sqsrte-text-color--black">Our Beebot Coding and Luka AI Reading Robots stimulate, engage and challenge our students to make learning both effective and fun. </span></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.335294s;"><strong>Signature programmes</strong> <span class="sqsrte-text-color--black">include Applied Learning Programme (ALP), K2 Space Buds Programme and Proprietary Music Curriculum developed by Methodist School of Music.</span></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.344118s;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--black">Our unique ALP presents learning as a challenging, engaging, and rewarding experience that fosters creative and critical thinking and practise the skills necessary to excel in project-based environments. ALP modules include Bee Bot, Key to Learning, Minecraft Education and Strawbees, and upcoming 3D Doodler and Blokies.</span></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.352941s;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--black">Our signature Space Buds programme is specially designed to introduce the K2 cohort to all things space and fire up a lifelong interest and foundational knowledge in space, while learning about STEM through a purposeful and intentional approach. Highlights of the Space Buds programme include an opportunity to zoom meet and interact with an astronaut and sample space ice cream!</span></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.361765s;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--black">We adopt</span> <strong>play-based, inquiry- and project-based learning approaches</strong> <span class="sqsrte-text-color--black">suited to age appropriateness as our preschoolers transit from pre-nursery to kindergarten levels to stimulate childrens affinity to curiosity, exploration, discovery and creativity  </span></p><p class="preFade" data-rte-preserve-empty="true" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.370588s;"></p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div><div class="sqs-block button-block sqs-block-button" data-block-type="53" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1645077256428_6542"><div class="sqs-block-content" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711868129119_251">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.405882s;" class="preSlide">Our Team and Learning Environment</h2><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.414706s;">At every Methodist preschool, we believe that every child deserves the best education. Our <span class="sqsrte-text-color--accent"><strong>dedicated team of educators is qualified, experienced and passionate</strong></span> about helping each child reach their full potential. We provide a caring, nurturing and <span class="sqsrte-text-color--accent"><strong>conducive learning environment</strong> </span>where every child feels loved, valued, and secure as they learn in well-equipped classrooms and facilities. </p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.423529s;">Our highly qualified curriculum specialists regularly review and enhance our curriculum to meet the evolving learning needs of the next generation in tandem with the latest developments in education. We are committed to providing your child with the best resources and opportunities for joyful and confident learning. </p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.432353s;">Give your child the gift of a quality education. Enrol them in our Methodist Preschool today!</p>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.458824s;" class="preSlide">School-Home-Community Synergy</h2><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.467647s;">At Methodist preschools, we place great emphasis on harnessing <span class="sqsrte-text-color--accent"><strong>school-home-community synergy</strong></span> in our childrens learning and development. We partner parents and caregivers to facilitate integration of learning in school and at home. We seek also Values-in-Action opportunities through involving our preschoolers in meaningful community involvement initiatives. </p>
</div>

<!-- Add Section IDs for anchor links -->
<script>
(function () {
  window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    var sections = document.querySelectorAll('section');
    var windowPath = window.location.pathname;
    // If page is set to homepage then set the anchor to home. i.e. #home-1
    if (windowPath === '/') {
      windowPath = 'home';
    }

    var anchorID = windowPath.replace('/', '');

    sections.forEach((section, i) => {
      section.id = `${anchorID}-${i+1}`;
    })
  })
})()
</script>

<script>
window.onscroll = function() {myFunction()};

function myFunction() {
  var winScroll = document.body.scrollTop || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
  var height = document.documentElement.scrollHeight - document.documentElement.clientHeight;
  var scrolled = (winScroll / height) * 100;
  document.getElementById("progressBar").style.width = scrolled + "%";
}
</script>
